function afterModuleLoaded() {
	
	Site.initPage2();
Site.initPageDesign(true,0,-1,0, 0);
Site.initPageAuth(true,-1000,0);
	

	
		Site.cacheModuleFunc.runManageInit();
		Site.cacheModuleFunc.runSiteInit();
		Site.dblclickUtils.init(); // 双击模块进入样式设置
	
	
	
	
			Site.demandLoadJs('//1.ss.faisys.com/js/comm/SWFUpload2v/swfupload.min.js?v=201711250202');
	
			Site.demandLoadJs('//1.ss.faisys.com/js/city2.min.js?v=201710231308');
	
			Site.demandLoadJs('//1.ss.faisys.com/js/comm/jquery/jquery-menu-aim.min.js?v=201711071637');
	
	
	

	
	    Site.currentProgress(100, function(){
	        $(".fk-loadingBar").remove();
	    });
	
} // afterModuleLoaded end

	});
	
	Site.loadCss("//2.ss.faisys.com/css/stylePanel.min.css?v=201712201616", function(){

	});
